<user_name>Justin Rimon< /user_name>< Text>
I did this for my birthday about two months ago and wow that was such a memorable and unique experience just an hour east of DTLA! The hike itself is already an adventure as you ford the San Gabriel river many times to arrive at this historic bridge. Trekking through the canyon is so beautiful too. I can't say enough about the Bungee America staff, we had an awesome person named Alex who gave the whole group a prep talk before we started the hike and got everyone super amped up and gave some cool history about the area.

For the actual bungee jump experience, it was both exhilarating and terrifying at the same time but I felt completely safe doing it. YOU GOTTA DO IT, it made me feel alive!! I did the two jump package which is the way to go since both jumps are a way different experience - did the superman front dive and the backwards starfish. Also it was really awesome meeting Ron, the founder of Bungee America and he was actually very involved with everything from safety protocol and keeping the energy high. Highly recommend doing this! It's one you won't forget :)</Text>

<text>My 2 friends surprised me for my birthday with bungee jumping. The hike starts early in the morning. The day I happened to go, they tried something different with who gets to jump first. If you had got there early for check in you had priority to jump, vs if you got there late, you were the last of the group to jump. I recommend getting there as early as possible because parking can be difficult and it‚Äôs usually a big group that jumps so you‚Äôd wait about 1-2 hours before you can jump if you‚Äôre checking in late. On the hike to the bridge, you‚Äôll pass the waterfall several times so maybe take extra socks and shoes that are comfortable and you don‚Äôt care about. There is a short break in between the hike. Once you get to the bridge you‚Äôll attend bungee jumping school where they teach you the safety of jumping and some cool and fun stories. Some of the stories include world records they been a part of. Be sure to pay attention because there are rules to ensure you have a safe, amazing, Instagram worthy jump. All of the staff made me feel beyond safe, were very polite and easy to talk to. You might decide to jump more than once when you get up there & you can do so. I highly recommend it though because Every jump is different. Each staff double checks you‚Äôre tied to your harness correctly and will even tell you what is the purpose for each buckle. After your jump, you‚Äôll receive a t shirt as a token for jumping. Since the staff alone made me feel safe i will 100% go again. The hike is overall 10 miles (to the bridge and back) it is beautiful, you might see big horn sheep and snakes on the way. be careful it can get a little steep at times. Take water and some snacks. Don‚Äôt hesitate to jump with bungee America at the bridge to nowhere. You wont regret it!ü§ôüèº</text>< time>

<rate>1< /rate>< review>
We had a great time hiking up to the bridge and back. My wife purchased two jumps for her and I. Our guide Chris was amazing, funny and understanding with everyone who feared taking the leap. He made us feel comfortable and safe. I almost chickened out and came back over the ledge where Chris convinced me and calmed my nerves and I took the jump twice. I‚Äôm not going to lie I‚Äôm torn on giving the amount of stars that I‚Äôm giving because overall we had a good time but I want this Review to be seen.

We had the ‚Äúluxury‚Äù to sit through three of Ron‚Äôs speeches with three groups. From 6am to 5pm. I say luxury because he chose my wife last to take the jump for the 6am team. When my wife showed fear he made no attempt to help her out or calm her instead he was rude to her by telling her that the reason he made her go last was because he knew she wasn‚Äôt going to jump. When my wife said ok just give me a chance he told her no. He made her get out of the gear and walked away. After her telling him ‚Äúyou‚Äôre really not going to give me a chance‚Äù he replied fine I‚Äôll give you another chance but we had to wait until what turned out to be the end of the day.

I get you have many people trying to jump and you have a business to run but you have to understand that people signed up because they want to do it but the fear to do it is real. I almost gave up and it took Chris a minute to calm my nerve. I also overheard Ron tell one of your crew members that the people who show fear ruin it for everyone else and that‚Äôs why you pick people who you think won‚Äôt show fear in the beginning to start the day so others would follow, which i understand but people are not paying for a cheap service so I think you owe them a bit of understanding.

Ron I know many people love you and the opportunity you offer but you can be a bit more human and understanding. I say more human because like I said earlier we had the opportunity to hear three of your speeches and I realize you are a good actor because you show emotion in what you do but everything you said was repetitive including your laugh and your hand movements. So much that I could pretty much could do the speech for you.

Anyway my low stars is not to discourage anyone from taking the hike or taking the jump in fact it was a great experience up until our experience with Ron.

Great job to Chris!!!< /review>

<userid>102946230477629129966</userid>< user_name>
Dana Alt</user_name>
<date>1608513532526</date><Rating>5</Rating>< Text>
Had a great experience with Bungee America! The staff is very knowledgeable and employs the use of multiple safeguards in their processes and procedures. They do a thorough job of explaining the equipment to jumpers and emphasizing what jumpers can do to get the best bungee jump.

The staff did inform us that there was a meeting time to get together with the entire group to hike out to the Bridge to Nowhere. The pace is about a mile in 20 minutes. It is best to keep in mind that this is not moderate terrain, and you will get a cardio workout out of this hike at this pace. If someone doesn't want to move at this pace or isn't able to, then they don't have to. People are able to hike out to the Bridge to Nowhere at their own pace and sign up for a jump at the bridge.

The people running this business did not turn anyone away from jumping. If they were at the bridge and wanted to jump, then they were able to sign up to jump that same day. This company wants people to have a good time and, most importantly, to be safe doing so. You won't find a better crew anywhere in the states. Hope you enjoy!<//Text>

<rate>2< /rate><Pics>None< /Pics><Gmap_id>0x80c28eb661a35507:0xaeafebe4754f3cd7</Gmap_id>< Text>
I don't think I've written a review in ages, but this experience has prompted me to write one.  I was SO excited for bungee jumping.  I was in the state for a conference and made my way down the coast.  I was doing some research and came across this organization.  Afterwards, I continued my research in order to figure out whether or not I wanted to jump with them.  Everything seemed to check out.

The site stated that there was a five mile hike---OK, no worries.  I like hiking & I like exploring.  The weekend prior I was in Yosemite, and I was fine.  On my way down the coast, I did some adventuring as well.

However, despite combing the website to see if there was something that I missed AND talking to who I believe is the gentleman who owns the place, I was not informed that the hike was at a fast-pace.

I'm not from the West.  Hiking for me includes lots of grass, dirt, and trees.  Not huge rocks and possibilities of falling to one's death (ironic, since we were going bungee jumping--I know).  SO I want to make sure I'm hiking purposefully in order to get through--not jumping effortlessly around like Indiana Jones.

As an aside--I weigh only about 170-80 and am regularly active.

Despite waking up real early and making my way over there, and despite starting the hike with everybody, I had to turn back.  I was trailing behind & couldn't keep up at all.  I physically couldn't keep up.  The guide kept telling me to go faster, but I could only go so fast!

I turned around.  Nobody even attempted to let me know how to figured out how to refund my money (this was a splurge after all).  I was SO disappointed.  I really wanted to go bungee jumping.

I'm sure the jumping part is fine, but getting there . . . . . unless you grew up in the area & can easily hop around, you're not gonna keep up.  :-(< /Text>

After several great dinners here last winter, I'm glad to report that the food, wine, ambiance, and service are all fantastic this winter.   Our friends who have introduced us to many great restaurants in SF were impressed.  There is no doubt I'll be back multiple times this winter.

< time>
1535493075281</time>
<Rating>3<//Rating>< Text>
Ever had your wedding cake redecorated in front of your eyes by an entitled stranger?! Thanks to a Christy Hill employee, we have!

On August 14th we took our intimate wedding party to Christy Hill for dinner after our ceremony where an older woman who seemed to be associated with the host stand or (god-forbid) management helped bring out our cake. Apparently not satisfied with the fun, self-decorating job we did along with our friends (we had a very free, easy, goofy wedding), she proceeded to pick leaves off of a nearby bush and add them to the layers of our cake. Next thing I noticed, she had procured some flowers from somewhere and started adding them, too. At this point I had to tell her that we were happy with the decoration job that was done - that's why we had done it - and that she could stop now. You could see the woman struggling to comprehend why we wouldn't want her to put the rest of the flowers and leaves in her hands on the cake. I gave her another "It's fine, you can stop" or something of the sort, and she she finally stepped away.

I cannot imagine a a world in which  someone would ever think it okay to redecorate someone else's wedding cake without their permission, but that's apparently the world this lady lives in, and she works at Christy Hill.

Also, even with the confirmation call they gave us that day, the one that I had placed a week prior, and the original call to make the reservation months before, they still got it wrong. We were a party of ten total and had asked for a table for eight for the wedding party and a nearby table for two for the photographer and videographer. When we arrived they had set the main table for ten, with a small table for two nearby, a total of twelve seats. Almost immediately we were asked if we didn't need the small table so they could give it to someone else since we could fit at the main table. Of course, we weren't going to say that our videographer and photographer needed to sit at the other table while the extra two spots at the main table sat empty; that seemed quite rude and awkward. There was an extra two-top table added to the main one that easily could have been left out, so I'm not sure if this was a tactic to get that other table back or what. Thankfully, our videographer and photographer were amazing additions to our day so it wasn't weird to have them dine with us!

I cannot deny, though, that the food was delicious. Our waiter was kind, the water and wine continuously refilled, and the bill ended up being less than expected! I still recommend going, maybe just don't choose this location for an event.< /Text>

<GmapID>0x80997d75ae9c3b7f:0xc771b005985f0e97<//GmapID><username>Andrew Wang<//username><Rating>5< /Rating><Time>1536122249695<//Time>< Text>
This restaurant is excellence and opulence beyond anything that can be comprehended, everything from the stunning eastward view of the lake, to the Seasonal Sorbet, everything was amazing. It is no wonder why this restaurant consistently ranks high among other restaurants in this caliber.  I was very pleased with the service provided, as despite not being dressed for the occasion or having a reservation, the front desk was pleasant and accommodating.

The food:

As a whole, the price point was reasonable for the service, view, and quality of food received, if you are making a decision simply based on this alone.

I ordered the Heirloom Tomato & Watermelon salad,  Deviled Green Eggs and Ham, the House Soup, the Pan Roasted Gnocchi, and finally the Fresh Tagliatelle Pasta.

The Heirloom Tomato & Watermelon salad was excellent, it is an excellent starter to share with a party of four. The colors really pop in this dish, and the taste of the tomatoes were well pronounced in this specific dish, as this salad brings together aspects of the sunflower and the tomato without it feeling forced. The sunflower seeds offered a nice aftertaste and fresh crunch to rely on, and the cilantro ver jus brought together the tomato and the sunflower elements in a harmonious alliance. It was not too acidic to overwhelm the flavors of the tomato, rather it complimented the freshly prepared tomato. To top the entire flavor profile, the Fromage Blanc was simply enthralling, not too pronounced to be the leading taste profile in the composition, but it had a unique presence that further brings all elements of the salad together.

In general, I am not usually a fan of deviled eggs, but the idea of this dish thought up by Dr. Seuss was too much to resist. First of all, the duck meat was sublime. The tiny strip of duck meat was just enough to give the appetizer the kick it needed, and I think it really compliments the entire dish very well. The taste of the duck and the watercress yolk mixture was out of this world. A point that perhaps was not to my liking was how undercooked the hard boiled egg, but perhaps that lends to how rich and creamy the watercress yolk was.

I honestly do not remember what the house soup was, but I do remember it was served intentionally cold, and that it was pretty good. It was a chicken stock based, and it was very smooth.

The Pan Roasted Gnocchi was really something else. First of all, the gnocchi was well cooked and the char on the outside allowed it to resist the moisture of the pan sauce, as the inside of the gnocchi was immersed enough with the sauce but the gnocchi held its shape well. The inside of the gnocchi was just barely permeated by the pan sauce, and the  poached egg also helped add dimension to the dish. The dish was very balanced with the proper ratio of vegetables and that allowed for an melodious dish. Again the duck meat in this dish was amazing. The meat was very tender as it barely clung to the fork as I went for the gnocchi. It was a pleasant surprise to see such a seemingly unconventional dish come together so nicely.

Despite the Fresh Tagliatelle Pasta being the most inexpensive of the pastas offered, it did not take away at all from the fact that this was the most memorable part of the dinner for me. I can still remember the texture of the pasta, the aroma of the mushroom ragout, and the lingering taste that the pine nuts in this harmonious amalgamation of all these locally sourced ingredients tossed with truffle oil. The large cuts of parmesan, peas, and the poached egg all everything that makes pasta unforgettable.  If anything on the menu was a must have, it would be this.

Everything on this menu goes above and beyond, and pushes the boundaries of fine cuisine in California. The creativity, innovation, and presentation is ethereal.</Text>

We returned to our favorite Tahoe City restaurant and were pleased again.  This is an exceptional restaurant in a beautiful lake side setting.  We ate a number of appetizers and small plates.   Initially, we started with salt roasted marble (colored round) potatoes served with an aioli.  If you like roasted potatoes, you will love these. Next, we shared deviled eggs with small slices of prosciutto garnish.  The charcuterie plate was superb.  Three cold pates, goose, chicken and a country style, with multiple mustards, pickled green strawberries, with Apple slices, dates and prosciutto garnishes. Finally, the seared fois gras was perfect as always.  The main dishes are varied, each with unique and interesting ingredients.  You will have a wonderful experience.  Enjoy the view from the deck or the main restaurant above.< /text>

-Update -

I ordered a Tohatsu outboard motor from Inflatable Boats online.  They called to verify my order was correct and promptly shipped the motor form California to Nebraska.  They provided a FedEx tracking number to follow shipment.  When the shipment arrived, the FedEx package was damaged and two plastic parts on the motor were broken. It is rare to find a company online who work so hard to deliver what they promise and stand behind their products.   I would definitely recommend Inflatable Boat Specialists for your boating needs!<//Review>

<text>We dealt with Brently, Frankie and Casey and all three of them couldn't have been nicer - patient, courteous and very helpful throughout the whole process

We were shopping for a new dinghy to replace our 25 year old Novurania RIB which finally died.  When we first came to the store Brently helped us look at used trade-ins and they had a number to choose from.  We chose a one year old Achilles with an aluminum floor, inflatable keel and bimini.  While this was not a RIB, we thought we would be OK with the aluminum floor and arranged to pick it up 3 days later with our trailer.

Before we picked it up we changed our mind and decided we wanted another RIB and we decided it would be new.  No problem to switch our deposit to a new one.  Frankie was particularly helpful explaining the pros/cons of Achilles vs Zodiac vs AB Inflatables.  He was also very patient going over the various models of each manufacturer in the size we were considering.  Once we settled on the Achilles 315DX, he quoted us a very fair price.  I compared his prices with a number of Achilles dealers between San Diego, LA and the Bay Area and he was $25 below the lowest quote I received on the phone.  Frankie was also helpful with the DMV paperwork and getting just the right color for the CF numbers keeping me informed along the way.

When we picked it about a week later Casey was a gem as our trailer rollers had to be adjusted for the shape of the Achilles hull.  He arranged for one of the mechanics to make the adjustments while we waited.  He also patiently explained all the major components and features.

Overall, one of the most pleasant purchasing experiences my wife and I have had!<//text><date>1493752430684</date>< Name>

<date>1606770109368</date><text>I was very skeptical on sending in my drone after it crashed and the gimbal was removed from the original position. I bought the DJI Care Refresh package as well when I bought the DJI Mavic Air 2, so I felt a little better about sending it in.

<user>101229583859283059522< /user><username>Garfield Adams aka J. Stemmons</username>< Date>
1383456467964< /Date>
<rating>5<//rating>< Review>
I initially went to Vape Mastaz because my usual spot I hit was out of the Kanthal gauge I was looking for.

I walked in and the vibe of the spot clicked with me instantly: turntables, various toys, mods and other vape essentials and the service was very disarming, informative and transparent (Nick was cool enough to admit that he didn't have much experience in a certain area...and the honesty was appreciated).  After discussing sub-ohm vaping, vape safety and a variety of build techniques they set me up with some 28 gauge Kanthal and a couple of their pre-rolled, pre-oxidized 400 Stainless Steel mesh sticks. I came home and with what I got at VM and some Eco Wool I already owned built a pretty nice 4 wrap coil (eco wool over ss mesh) that is reading at 1.11 ohms and I'm SUPER hype!

The retail space is small and there wasn't any sitting room, but the spot is still pretty fresh and worth checking out if you don't wanna drive to Alhambra, San Gabriel or any other southern San Gabriel Valley city for vape needs. Nothing wrong with those cities, it just feels good to have some quality vape joints up this way in Pasadena!

Thanks, fellas!

Peace.<//Review>
